      <!--PROfilePageNumberReset%Num%2%%%-->
      <div style="text-align: center; font-family: Arial; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF RESTRICTED STOCK UNIT AWARD</div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">1.</font>&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>General</u></font>.&#160; These Terms and Conditions of Restricted Stock Unit Award (these &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Terms</u></font>&#8221;) apply to a particular restricted stock unit award (the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Award</u></font>&#8221;) granted by Apple Inc., a California corporation (the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Company</u></font>&#8221;), and are incorporated by reference in the Notice
          of Grant (the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Grant Notice</u></font>&#8221;) corresponding to that particular grant.&#160; The recipient of the Award identified in the Grant Notice is referred to as the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Non-Employee Director</u></font>.&#8221;&#160; The effective date of grant of the Award as set forth in the Grant Notice is referred to as the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Award Date</u></font>.&#8221;&#160; The
          Award was granted under and is subject to the provisions of the Apple Inc. Non-Employee Director Stock Plan, as amended and restated on November 4, 2025 (the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Plan</u></font>&#8221;).&#160; Capitalized
          terms are defined in the Plan if not defined herein.&#160; The Award has been granted to the Non-Employee Director in addition to, and not in lieu of, any other form of compensation otherwise payable or to be paid to the Non-Employee Director.&#160; The
          Grant Notice and these Terms are collectively referred to as the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Award Agreement</u></font>&#8221; applicable to the Award.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">2.</font>&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Stock Units</u></font>.&#160; As used herein, the term &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Stock Unit</u></font>&#8221; shall mean a non-voting unit of measurement which is deemed for bookkeeping purposes to be equivalent to
          one outstanding share of the Company&#8217;s Common Stock (&#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Share</u></font>&#8221;) solely for purposes of the Plan and this Award Agreement.&#160; The Stock Units shall be used solely as a device for the
          determination of the payment to eventually be made to the Non-Employee Director if such Stock Units vest pursuant to this Award Agreement.&#160; The Stock Units shall not be treated as property or as a trust fund of any kind.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">3.</font>&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Vesting</u></font>.&#160; Subject to Section 8 below and Section 4 of the Plan, the Award shall vest and become nonforfeitable as set forth in the Grant Notice.&#160; The vesting date set forth in the Grant Notice or the date on which the award
          otherwise vests in accordance with Section 8(b) below is referred to herein as the &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Vesting Date</u></font>.&#8221;</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">4.</font>&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Continuance of Service</u></font>.&#160; The vesting of the Award requires continued service as a member of the Board through the Vesting Date as a condition to the vesting of the Award and the rights and benefits under this Award
          Agreement.&#160; Service as a member of the Board for only a portion of the vesting period, even if a substantial portion, will not entitle the Non-Employee Director to any proportionate vesting or avoid or mitigate a termination of rights and
          benefits upon or following a termination of service as provided in Section 8 below and in the Plan.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 72pt; font-family: Arial; font-size: 10pt;">Nothing contained in this Award Agreement or the Plan shall be deemed to create any obligation on the part of the Board to nominate any of its members for
        reelection by the Company&#8217;s shareholders, nor confer upon the Non-Employee Director the right to remain a member of the Board for any period of time, or at any particular rate of compensation.&#160; Nothing in this Section 4, however, is intended to
        adversely affect any independent contractual right of the Non-Employee Director without his or her consent thereto.</div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">5.</font>&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Dividend and Voting Rights</u></font>.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 72pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">&#160;(a)</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Limitations


              on Rights Associated with Stock Units</u></font>.&#160; The Non-Employee Director shall have no rights as a shareholder of the Company, no dividend rights (except as expressly provided in Section 5(b) with respect to Dividend Equivalent Rights)
          and no voting rights with respect to the Stock Units or any Shares underlying or issuable in respect of such Stock Units until such Shares are actually issued to and held of record by the Non-Employee Director.&#160; No adjustments will be made for
          dividends or other rights of a holder for which the record date is prior to the date upon which the Non-Employee Director will become the holder of record thereof.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div class="BRPFPageBreakArea" style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;">
        <div style="text-align: center;" class="BRPFPageNumberArea"><font style="font-family: Arial; font-size: 8pt; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;">2</font></div>
        <div class="BRPFPageBreak" style="page-break-after: always;">
          <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 72pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">&#160;(b)</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Dividend


              Equivalent Rights</u></font>.&#160; As of any date that the Company pays an ordinary cash dividend on its Common Stock, the Company shall credit the Non-Employee Director with a dollar amount equal to (i) the per share cash dividend paid by the
          Company on its Common Stock on such date, multiplied by (ii) the total number of Stock Units (with such total number adjusted pursuant to Section 7 of the Plan) subject to the Award that are outstanding on the record date for that dividend (a &#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Dividend Equivalent Right</u></font>&#8221;).&#160; Any Dividend Equivalent Rights credited pursuant to the foregoing provisions of this Section 5(b) shall be subject to the same vesting, payment and other
          terms, conditions and restrictions as the original Stock Units to which they relate; provided, however, that the amount of any vested Dividend Equivalent Rights shall be paid in cash.&#160; No crediting of Dividend Equivalent Rights shall be made
          pursuant to this Section 5(b) with respect to any Stock Units which, immediately prior to the record date for that dividend, have either been paid pursuant to Section 7 or terminated pursuant to Section 8.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">6.</font>&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Restrictions on Transfer</u></font>.&#160; Except as provided in Section 6 of the Plan, the Award, the Dividend Equivalent Rights and any interest therein or amount or Shares payable in respect thereof shall not be sold, assigned,
          transferred, pledged or otherwise disposed of, alienated or encumbered, either voluntarily or involuntarily.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">7.</font>&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Timing and Manner of Payment of Stock Units</u></font>.&#160; On or as soon as administratively practical following the Vesting Date (and in all events not later than two and one-half (2 &#189;) months after the Vesting Date), the Company shall
          deliver to the Non-Employee Director a number of Shares <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">(as evidenced by an appropriate entry on the books of the Company or a duly authorized transfer agent of the Company) </font>equal to the
          number of Stock Units subject to the Award that vest on the Vesting Date.&#160; The Non-Employee Director shall have no further rights with respect to any Stock Units that are so paid or that terminate pursuant to Section 8(a).</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">8.</font>&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Effect of Termination of Service</u></font>.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 72pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">&#160;(a)</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">If the Non-Employee Director ceases to serve as a member of the Board for
          any reason other than death, the Stock Units (as well as the related Dividend Equivalent Rights) shall terminate to the extent such Stock Units have not become vested prior to the first date the Non-Employee Director is no longer a member of the
          Board, and the Non-Employee Director will have no rights with respect to, or in respect of, such terminated Stock Units.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 72pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">&#160;(b)</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; &#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;">If the Non-Employee Director ceases to serve as a member of the Board due to
          his or her death, the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s unvested Stock Units shall fully vest as of the date of the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s death.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">9.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Adjustments Upon Specified Events</u></font>.&#160; Upon the occurrence of certain events relating to the Company&#8217;s stock contemplated by Section 7 of the Plan, the Board shall make adjustments in accordance with such section in the number
          of Stock Units then outstanding and the number and type of securities that may be issued in respect of the Award.&#160; No such adjustment shall be made with respect to any ordinary cash dividend for which Dividend Equivalent Rights are credited
          pursuant to Section 5(b).</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div class="BRPFPageBreakArea" style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;">
        <div style="text-align: center;" class="BRPFPageNumberArea"><font style="font-family: Arial; font-size: 8pt; font-weight: normal; font-style: normal;">3</font></div>
        <div class="BRPFPageBreak" style="page-break-after: always;">
          <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">10.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Responsibility for Taxes</u></font>.&#160; The Non-Employee Director agrees to report and pay any and all income tax, social insurance, or payroll taxes (&#8220;<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><u>Tax-Related Items</u></font>&#8221;)
          that arise as a result of the grant, vesting or settlement of the Award, the subsequent sale of any Shares acquired at vesting and the receipt of any dividends or Dividend Equivalent Rights.&#160; The Company is not responsible for withholding with
          regard to the Tax-Related Items.&#160; However, the Company reserves the right to withhold any Tax-Related Items to the extent circumstances change and it is required to do so.&#160; In this regard, the Non-Employee Director authorizes the Company, at its
          discretion and pursuant to such procedures as it may specify from time to time, to satisfy any withholding obligations with regard to all Tax-Related Items by one or a combination of the following methods: (a) withholding from cash amounts
          otherwise payable to the Non-Employee Director by the Company; (b) withholding otherwise deliverable Shares or from otherwise payable Dividend Equivalent Rights to be issued or paid upon settlement of the Award (c) arranging for the sale of
          Shares otherwise deliverable to the Non-Employee Director (on the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s behalf and at the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s direction pursuant to this authorization), including selling Shares as part of a block trade with other
          participants in the Plan or other plans of the Company; or (d) withholding from the proceeds of the sale of Shares acquired upon settlement of the Award.&#160; The Company may refuse to distribute the Shares or other property credited to the
          Non-Employee Director if the Non-Employee Director fails to comply with the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s obligations in connection with the Tax-Related Items as described in this Section 10.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">11.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Electronic Delivery and Acceptance</u></font>.&#160; The <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Company may, in its sole discretion, deliver any documents related to the Award by electronic means or
            request the </font>Non-Employee <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Director&#8217;s consent to participate in the Plan by electronic means.&#160; The </font>Non-Employee <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Director hereby consents to receive all applicable documentation by electronic delivery and to participate in the Plan through an online or voice activated system established and maintained by the Company or a third
            party vendor designated by the Company.</font></font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">12.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Data Privacy</u></font>.&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">The Non-Employee Director acknowledges and consents to the collection, use, processing and transfer of personal data as described in
            this Section 12.&#160; The Company and its related entities may hold certain personal information about the Non-Employee Director, including the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s name, home address and telephone number, date of birth, social security number
            or other identification number, compensation, nationality, job title, any Shares or directorships held in the Company, details of all options or any other entitlement to Shares awarded, canceled, purchased, vested, unvested or outstanding in
            the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s favor (&#8220;<u>Data</u>&#8221;), for the purpose of managing and administering the Plan.&#160; The Company and its related entities may transfer Data amongst themselves as necessary for the purpose of implementation,
            administration, and management of the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s participation in the Plan, and the Company and its related entities may each further transfer Data to any third parties assisting the Company or any such related entity in the
            implementation, administration, and management of the Plan.&#160; The Non-Employee Director acknowledges that the transferors and transferees of such Data may be located anywhere in the world and hereby authorizes each of them to receive, possess,
            use, retain, and transfer the Data, in electronic or other form, for the purposes of implementing, administering, and managing the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s participation in the Plan, including any transfer of such Data as may be required for the
            administration of the Plan or the subsequent holding of Shares on the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s behalf to a broker or to other third party with whom the Non-Employee Director may elect to deposit any Shares acquired under the Plan (whether
            pursuant to the Award or otherwise).</font></font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">13.</font>&#160; <u></u><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Notices</u></font>.&#160; Any notice to be given under the terms of this Award Agreement shall be in writing and addressed to the Company at its principal office to the attention of the Secretary, and to the Non-Employee
          Director at the Non-Employee Director&#8217;s last address reflected on the Company&#8217;s records, or at such other address as either party may hereafter designate in writing to the other.&#160; Any such notice shall be given only when received, but if the
          Non-Employee Director is no longer a member of the Board, shall be deemed to have been duly given by the Company when enclosed in a properly sealed envelope addressed as aforesaid, registered or certified, and deposited (postage and registry or
          certification fee prepaid) in a post office or branch post office regularly maintained by the United States Government.</font></div>

      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">14.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Plan</u></font>.&#160; The Award and all rights of the Non-Employee Director under this Award Agreement are subject to the terms and conditions of the provisions of the Plan, which is incorporated herein by reference.&#160; The Non-Employee
          Director agrees to be bound by the terms of the Plan and this Award Agreement.&#160; The Non-Employee Director acknowledges having read and understood the Plan and this Award Agreement.&#160; Unless otherwise expressly provided in other sections of this
          Award Agreement, provisions of the Plan that confer discretionary authority on the Board do not (and shall not be deemed to) create any rights in the Non-Employee Director unless such rights are expressly set forth herein or are otherwise in the
          sole discretion of the Board so conferred by appropriate action of the Board under the Plan after the date hereof.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">15.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Entire Agreement</u></font>.&#160; This Award Agreement and the Plan together constitute the entire agreement and supersede all prior understandings and agreements, written or oral, of the parties hereto with respect to the subject matter
          hereof.&#160; The Plan and this Award Agreement may be amended pursuant to Section 10 of the Plan. The Company may, however, unilaterally waive any provision hereof in writing to the extent such waiver does not adversely affect the interests of the
          Non-Employee Director hereunder, but no such waiver shall operate as or be construed to be a subsequent waiver of the same provision or a waiver of any other provision hereof.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">16.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Limitation on the Non-Employee Director</u><u>&#8217;s Rights</u></font>.&#160; Participation in the Plan<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">&#160;</font>confers no<font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">&#160;</font>rights or interests other than as herein provided.&#160; This Award Agreement creates only a contractual obligation on the part of the Company as to amounts payable and shall not be construed as creating a trust.&#160; Neither
          the Plan nor any underlying program, in and of itself, has any assets.&#160; The Non-Employee Director shall have only the rights of a general unsecured creditor of the Company with respect to amounts credited and benefits payable, if any, with
          respect to the Stock Units, and rights no greater than the right to receive the Common Stock as a general unsecured creditor with respect to Stock Units, as and when payable hereunder.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">17.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Counterparts</u></font>.&#160; This Award Agreement may be executed simultaneously in any number of counterparts, each of which shall be deemed an original but all of which together shall constitute one and the same instrument.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">18.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Section Headings</u></font>.&#160; The section headings of this Award Agreement are for convenience of reference only and shall not be deemed to alter or affect any provision hereof.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">19.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Governing Law</u></font>.&#160; This Award Agreement shall be governed by and construed and enforced in accordance with the laws of the State of California and applicable U.S. federal laws without regard to conflict of law principles
          thereunder.</font></div>

      <div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;">20.</font>&#160; <font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; font-weight: bold;"><u>Choice of Venue</u></font>.&#160; For purposes of litigating any dispute that arises directly or indirectly from the relationship of the parties evidenced by this grant or this Award Agreement, the parties hereby submit to the exclusive
          jurisdiction of the State of California and agree that such litigation shall be conducted only in the courts of Santa Clara County, California, or the federal courts for the Northern District of California, and no other courts, where this grant
          is made or to be performed.</font></div>
      <div>&#160;</div>

          that intent.</font></div>

          be binding and enforceable.</font></div>
